    63   const handlePointerDown = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    64     // 阻止默认行为，防止浏览器 context-menu / text-select / callout 干扰长按
    65     e.preventDefault();
    66     e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    67     startXRef.current = e.clientX;
    68     startYRef.current = e.clientY;
    69     longFiredRef.current = false;
    70     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    71     longTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
    72       longFiredRef.current = true;
    73       onLongPress?.(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    74     }, LONG_PRESS_MS);
    75   }, [onLongPress]);
    76 
    77   const handlePointerMove = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    78     if (dragStartedRef.current) return;
    79     const dx = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
    80     const dy = e.clientY - startYRef.current;
    81     if (Math.hypot(dx, dy) > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
    82       dragStartedRef.current = true;
    83       cancelLongPress();
    84       // 拖拽正式开始时立即释放指针捕获：
    85       // 若保留捕获，换页时 AppIcon 会从 DOM 卸载，浏览器因此触发 pointercancel 清除拖拽状态
    86       if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    87         e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    88       }
    89       onDragBegin?.(item, e.clientX, e.clientY);
    90     }
    91   }, [item, onDragBegin, cancelLongPress]);
    92 
    93   const handlePointerUp = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    94     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    95     cancelLongPress();
    96     // 确保释放捕获（未达到拖拽阈值时）
    97     if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    98       e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);

```
// 查找空白位置
function findEmptySlot(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage?: number,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
  const order = preferPage !== undefined
    ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);

  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < MAX_COLS; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```
New String: ```
// 查找空白位置（maxCols 限制实际渲染列数，避免图标放到不可见列）
function findEmptySlot(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage?: number,
  maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
  const order = preferPage !== undefined
    ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);

  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```

```
  const addItem = useCallback((
```

```
function findFirstEmpty(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
```

```
// 辅助：在 preferPage 上找第一个空格（跳过被拖拽项自身），用于边缘松手时的回退落点
function findFirstEmpty(
  pages: DesktopItem[][],
  preferPage: number,
  excludeId?: string,
  maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
  const order = [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)];
  for (const p of order) {
    for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
      if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
      for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
        const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c && it.id !== excludeId);
        if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}
```

    83 
    84 // 查找空白位置（maxCols 限制实际渲染列数，避免图标放到不可见列）
    85 function findEmptySlot(
    86   pages: DesktopItem[][],
    87   preferPage?: number,
    88   maxCols: number = MAX_COLS,
    89 ): { page: number; row: number; col: number } | null {
    90   // 从 preferPage 开始搜索，保证新应用优先出现在当前页
    91   const order = preferPage !== undefined
    92     ? [preferPage, ...Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i).filter(i => i !== preferPage)]
    93     : Array.from({ length: pages.length }, (_, i) => i);
    94 
    95   for (const p of order) {
    96     for (let r = 0; r < MAX_ROWS; r++) {
    97       // widget 独占整行，跳过该行所有列
    98       if (pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.type === 'widget')) continue;
    99       for (let c = 0; c < maxCols; c++) {
   100         const occupied = pages[p].some((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);
   101         if (!occupied) return { page: p, row: r, col: c };
   102       }
   103     }
   104   }
   105   return null;
   106 }
   107

Let me think of a simpler approach.\n\nAlternative for merge detection: instead of using `elementsFromPoint`, use `document.querySelector(\'[data-itemid]\')` to find all cells with items and check if the ghost center overlaps with any of them using `getBoundingClientRect()`.\n\nThis would be more reliable than `elementsFromPoint`.\n\n```tsx\n// Find which cell the ghost center is over\nconst ghosts = ghostRef.current;\nconst cx = e.clientX, cy = e.clientY;\nlet foundHoverId: string | null = null;\nconst cells = document.querySelectorAll(\'[data-itemid]\');\nfor (const cellEl of cells) {\n  const rect = cellEl.getBoundingClientRect();\n  if (cx >= rect.left && cx <= rect.right && cy >= rect.top && cy <= rect.bottom) {\n    foundHoverId = (cellEl as HTMLElement).dataset.itemid ?? null;\n    break;\n  }\n}\nconst hoverId = foundHoverId;\n```\n\nThis approach avoids all the `elementsFromPoint` ambiguity. It geometrically checks if the ghost center is within any cell\'s bounding rect. More reliable!\n\nSimilarly for `onUp`, we can use this approach to find the target cell.\n\nFor `onUp`, we need BOTH occupied and empty cells. We can query `[data-cell]` instead.\n\nTHIS IS THE CORRECT FIX. Let me replace the `elementsFromPoint` approach with geometry-based detection.\n\nActually, for `onUp`, the cell element already has both `data-cell` (for empty cells too) and `data-itemid` (for occupied cells). The `getBoundingClientRect` approach would work for both.\n\nLet me plan the rewrite:\n\n**onMove (hover for merge):**\n```tsx\n// Geometry-based hover detection: find item cell containing ghost center\nlet hoverId: string | null = null;\nconst itemCells = document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>(\'[data-cell][data-itemid]\');\nfor (const cellEl of itemCells) {\n  const r = cellEl.getBoundingClientRect();\n  if (e.clientX >= r.left && e.clientX <= r.right && e.clientY >= r.top && e.clientY <= r.bottom) {\n    hoverId = cellEl.dataset.itemid!;\n    break;\n  }\n}\n```\n\n**onUp (drop detection):**\n```tsx\n// Geometry-based drop detection: find cell (any, including empty) containing pointer\nlet cell: HTMLElement | null = null;\nconst allCells = document.querySelectorAll<HTMLElement>(\'[data-cell]\');\nfor (const cellEl of allCells) {\n  const r = cellEl.getBoundingClientRect();\n  if (e.clientX >= r.left && e.clientX <= r.right && e.clientY >= r.top && e.clientY <= r.bottom) {\n    cell = cellEl;\n    break;\n  }\n}\n```\n\nThis is more reliable than `elementsFromPoint`. `getBoundingClientRect()` always works correctly regardless of z-index, pointer-events, etc.\n\nAdditionally, for EDGE THRESHOLD fix: reduce from 36 to 8px.\n\nLet me now write the complete fix.\n\nAlso for the "icon disappears" issue: I think the problem might be specific to `latestRef`. Let me change `useEffect` to `useLayoutEffect` for the latestRef update to ensure it\'s always in sync before pointer events are processed.\n\nActually, I realize there\'s ONE MORE potential source of "icon disappears". When `onUp` is called and we find a cell, we might be finding a WRONG cell if the user lifts finger at the edge of a cell. `getBoundingClientRect` approach would find the cell EXACTLY, which is more reliable.\n\nBut could it fail? If the user\'s pointer is outside all cells (between cells, in gaps), `cell = null` → fallback to `findFirstEmpty`. The item moves to first empty slot, which might not be where user intended. This looks like "disappearing" if the first empty slot is off-screen or on another page.\n\nFIX for fallback: when no cell is found, DON\'T move the item (keep it at original position). This is safer than moving to a random slot.\n\nActually the current fallback does: `findFirstEmpty(d.pages, cp, g.source.itemId, gridCols)` which finds first empty on current page within gridCols. This should put the item in a visible position.\n\nUnless the current page is FULL. Then `findFirstEmpty` checks other pages. If the item ends up on page 1 but user is on page 0, the item appears to "disappear" (it\'s on a different page).\n\nFIX for this: when no cell is found, keep item at ORIGINAL POSITION (no move):\n```tsx\n} else {\n  // 未命中有效格子 → 保持原位\n  return; // or moveTo(id, src.page, src.page, src.row, src.col)\n}\n```\n\nThis is actually a much better UX - if you don\'t drop on a valid cell, the item just springs back to where it was.\n\nLet me now plan ALL the fixes:\n\n1. Replace `elementsFromPoint` with `getBoundingClientRect` in both `onMove` and `onUp`\n2. When no cell found in `onUp`: keep item at original position (no move)\n3. Reduce `EDGE_THRESHOLD` from 36 to 8\n4. Reduce `MERGE_DELAY` from 1500 to 800ms\n5. Change `useEffect` latestRef update to `useLayoutEffect`\n\nThese are comprehensive fixes that should address all three issues.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

     9 interface AppIconProps {
    10   item: DesktopItem;
    11   onClick?: () => void;
    12   onLongPress?: (x: number, y: number) => void;
    13   onDragBegin?: (item: DesktopItem, x: number, y: number) => void;

    21 const LONG_PRESS_MS = 500;
    22 // 手机端手指轻微抖动约 5-10px，阈值设为 14px 以避免误触取消长按
    23 const DRAG_THRESHOLD = 14;
    24 
    25 const AppIcon: React.FC<AppIconProps> = ({
    26   item, onClick, onLongPress, onDragBegin,
    27   onDeleteInEditMode, size = 'normal', ghost = false, iconPx,
    28 }) => {
    29   const { editMode, settings } = useDesktop();
    30   const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
    31   const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(false);
    32   // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL
    33   const [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>
    34     item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined
    35   );
    36 
    37   // item.iconUrl 变化时（编辑后）同步更新 iconSrc
    38   useEffect(() => {
    39     if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }
    40     setImgError(false);
    41     setImgLoaded(false);
    42     setIconSrc(getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl);
    43   }, [item.iconUrl]);
    44 
    45   const longTimerRef = useRef<ReturnType<typeof setTimeout> | null>(null);
    46   const longFiredRef  = useRef(false);
    47   const startXRef     = useRef(0);
    48   const startYRef     = useRef(0);
    49   const dragStartedRef = useRef(false);
    50 
    51   const isSmall = size === 'small';
    52   // 图标尺寸：small 固定, normal 使用 settings 或 iconPx 覆盖
    53   const px = isSmall ? 48 : (iconPx ?? settings.iconSize ?? 46);
    54   const textSize = isSmall ? 'text-[10px]' : 'text-[11px]';
    55 
    56   // 新拟态风格阴影
    57   const isNeumorphism = settings.style === 'neumorphism';
    58 
    59   const cancelLongPress = useCallback(() => {
    60     if (longTimerRef.current) { clearTimeout(longTimerRef.current); longTimerRef.current = null; }
    61   }, []);
    62 
    63   const handlePointerDown = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    64     // 阻止默认行为，防止浏览器 context-menu / text-select / callout 干扰长按
    65     e.preventDefault();
    66     e.currentTarget.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    67     startXRef.current = e.clientX;
    68     startYRef.current = e.clientY;
    69     longFiredRef.current = false;
    70     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    71     longTimerRef.current = setTimeout(() => {
    72       longFiredRef.current = true;
    73       onLongPress?.(e.clientX, e.clientY);
    74     }, LONG_PRESS_MS);
    75   }, [onLongPress]);
    76 
    77   const handlePointerMove = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    78     if (dragStartedRef.current) return;
    79     const dx = e.clientX - startXRef.current;
    80     const dy = e.clientY - startYRef.current;
    81     if (Math.hypot(dx, dy) > DRAG_THRESHOLD) {
    82       dragStartedRef.current = true;
    83       cancelLongPress();
    84       // 拖拽正式开始时立即释放指针捕获：
    85       // 若保留捕获，换页时 AppIcon 会从 DOM 卸载，浏览器因此触发 pointercancel 清除拖拽状态
    86       if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    87         e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    88       }
    89       onDragBegin?.(item, e.clientX, e.clientY);
    90     }
    91   }, [item, onDragBegin, cancelLongPress]);
    92 
    93   const handlePointerUp = useCallback((e: React.PointerEvent) => {
    94     dragStartedRef.current = false;
    95     cancelLongPress();
    96     // 确保释放捕获（未达到拖拽阈值时）
    97     if (e.currentTarget.hasPointerCapture(e.pointerId)) {
    98       e.currentTarget.releasePointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    99     }
   100   }, [cancelLongPress]);
   101 
   102   const handleClick = useCallback(() => {
   103     if (longFiredRef.current || dragStartedRef.current) return;
   104     if (editMode && item.type !== 'system') return;
   105     if (item.type === 'app' && item.url) window.open(item.url, '_blank', 'noopener,noreferrer');
   106     else onClick?.();
   107   }, [editMode, item, onClick]);
   108

   110     width: px, height: px,
   111     borderRadius: '22%',
   112     flexShrink: 0,
   113     ...(isNeumorphism ? {
   114       boxShadow: '4px 4px 10px rgba(0,0,0,0.12), -4px -4px 10px rgba(255,255,255,0.7)',
   115     } : {}),
   116   };
   117 
   118   const renderIconContent = () => {
   119     if (item.type === 'system') {
   120       const iconMap: Record<string, React.ElementType> = {
   121         'sys-settings': Settings, 'sys-sync': RefreshCw, 'sys-add': Plus,
   122       };
   123       const Icon = iconMap[item.id] ?? Globe;
   124       return (

   128         </div>
   129       );
   130     }
   131     if (item.type === 'folder') {
   132       // 取前 4 个子项，以 2×2 网格展示缩略图
   133       const preview = (item.children || []).slice(0, 4);
   134       const isNeu = settings.style === 'neumorphism';
   135       // 单个格子边长（去掉间距后均分）
   136       const cellPx = (px * 0.68 - 4) / 2; // gap=4px，共 1 条
   137       return (
   138         <div

   148           {preview.length > 0 ? (
   149             <div
   150               className="grid gap-[4px]"
   151               style={{
   152                 gridTemplateColumns: `repeat(2, ${cellPx}px)`,
   153                 gridTemplateRows: `repeat(2, ${cellPx}px)`,
   154               }}
   155             >
   156               {preview.map((child) => (
   157                 <div
   158                   key={child.id}
   159                   className="rounded-[18%] overflow-hidden flex items-center justify-center"
   160                   style={{
   161                     width: cellPx,
   162                     height: cellPx,
   163                     background: child.iconUrl ? 'transparent' : 'rgba(255,255,255,0.25)',
   164                     flexShrink: 0,
   165                   }}
   166                 >
   167                   {child.iconUrl ? (
   168                     <img
   169                       src={getIconCache(child.iconUrl) ?? child.iconUrl}
   170                       alt=""
   171                       draggable={false}
   172                       style={{ width: cellPx, height: cellPx, objectFit: 'cover', display: 'block' }}
   173                     />
   174                   ) : (
   175                     <span className="text-white font-bold drop-shadow" style={{ fontSize: px * 0.16 }}>
   176                       {child.name.slice(0, 1)}
   177                     </span>
   178                   )}
   179                 </div>
   180               ))}
   181             </div>
   182           ) : (
   183             <Folder style={{ width: px * 0.5, height: px * 0.5 }} className="text-white drop-shadow" />
   184           )}
   185         </div>
   186       );
   187     }
   188     if (iconSrc && !imgError) {
   189       return (
   190         <div
   191           className="overflow-hidden ios-icon-shadow relative"
   192           style={{
   193             ...iconStyle,
   194             background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   195             backdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   196             WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   197 
   198           }}
   199         >
   200           {/* 骨架屏：图片加载完成前显示 shimmer 动画 */}
   201           {!imgLoaded && (
   202             <div
   203               className="absolute inset-0 animate-skeleton-pulse"
   204               style={{ borderRadius: '22%', background: 'linear-gradient(90deg,rgba(200,200,200,0.3) 25%,rgba(220,220,220,0.5) 50%,rgba(200,200,200,0.3) 75%)', backgroundSize: '200% 100%' }}
   205             />
   206           )}
   207           <img
   208             src={iconSrc}
   209             alt={item.name}
   210             draggable={false}
   211             className="w-full h-full object-cover"
   212             style={{ opacity: imgLoaded ? 1 : 0, transition: 'opacity 0.2s ease' }}
   213             onLoad={() => {
   214               setImgLoaded(true);
   215               // 图片加载成功后，后台静默缓存为 DataURL；不修改 iconSrc 避免 src 变动闪白
   216               if (!item.iconUrl || iconSrc.startsWith('data:')) return;
   217               fetchAndCacheIcon(item.iconUrl); // fire-and-forget，下次挂载时从缓存读取
   218             }}
   219             onError={(e) => {
   220               const img = e.currentTarget;
   221               // 尝试直连 favicon.ico 作为回退
   222               if (item.url && !img.dataset.fallbackTried) {
   223                 img.dataset.fallbackTried = '1';
   224                 const fallback = getDirectFaviconUrl(normalizeUrl(item.url));
   225                 if (fallback && fallback !== iconSrc) { img.src = fallback; return; }
   226               }
   227               setImgError(true);
   228             }}
   229           />
   230         </div>
   231       );
   232     }
   233     return (
   234       <div
   235         className="flex items-center justify-center ios-icon-shadow"
   236         style={{
   237           ...iconStyle,
   238           background: 'rgba(255,255,255,0.18)',
   239           backdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   240           WebkitBackdropFilter: 'blur(16px)',
   241 
   242         }}
   243       >
   244         {item.url ? (
   245           <Globe style={{ width: px * 0.5, height: px * 0.5 }} className="text-white drop-shadow" />
   246         ) : (
   247           <span className="text-white font-bold uppercase drop-shadow" style={{ fontSize: px * 0.35 }}>{item.name.slice(0, 1)}</span>
   248         )}
   249       </div>
   250     );
   251   };
   252 
   253   return (
   254     <div className={`relative ${ghost ? 'opacity-40' : ''}`}>
   255       <button
   256         type="button"
   257         onClick={handleClick}
   258         onPointerDown={handlePointerDown}

   260         onPointerUp={handlePointerUp}
   261         onPointerCancel={handlePointerUp}
   262         onContextMenu={(e) => e.preventDefault()}
   263         className={`flex flex-col items-center gap-1 select-none touch-none ${editMode ? 'animate-wiggle' : ''} transition-transform active:scale-95`}
   264       >
   265         {renderIconContent()}
   266         <span
   267           className={`app-icon-label ${textSize} font-medium truncate ${isNeumorphism ? 'text-slate-600' : 'text-white drop-shadow-md'}`}
   268           style={{ maxWidth: px + 8 }}
   269         >
   270           {item.name}
   271         </span>
   272       </button>
   273       {editMode && item.type !== 'system' && onDeleteInEditMode && (
   274         <button
   275           type="button"
   276           onClick={(e) => { e.stopPropagation(); onDeleteInEditMode(item.id); }}
   277           className="absolute -top-1 -left-1 z-20 w-5 h-5 rounded-full bg-destructive flex items-center justify-center shadow-md"
   278           aria-label="删除"
   279         >
   280           <X className="w-3 h-3 text-white" strokeWidth={3} />
   281         </button>
   282       )}
   283     </div>
   284   );
   285 };
   286 
   287 export default AppIcon;

AgentThinkAction(thought='Now I understand the issue clearly. Looking at AppIcon.tsx:\n\nLine 30-35:\n```tsx\nconst [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(false);\nconst [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>\n  item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n);\n```\n\nThe problem is:\n1. `imgLoaded` starts as `false` \n2. The image has `opacity: imgLoaded ? 1 : 0` → starts invisible\n3. Until `onLoad` fires (which happens when the image finishes loading), the icon shows the skeleton shimmer\n\nBut here\'s the KEY ISSUE: every time `AppIcon` is **REMOUNTED** (which happens when:\n- Changing pages (items unmount/remount)\n- After drag/drop (data change causes re-render)\n\n...the component remounts with `imgLoaded = false` again. Even if the image is ALREADY LOADED by the browser (cached in HTTP cache), the component doesn\'t know this because React state is reset.\n\nWhen the component mounts:\n1. `imgLoaded = false` → image `opacity: 0`\n2. Browser immediately loads from HTTP cache\n3. `onLoad` fires → `imgLoaded = true` → opacity: 1\n\nBut there\'s a potential issue: if the browser already has the image in cache, `onLoad` fires synchronously (or very quickly), BUT React state update is async. So there\'s a brief moment where `imgLoaded = false`.\n\nActually, the more important issue: `iconSrc` is initialized as:\n```tsx\n() => item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n```\n\n`getIconCache(item.iconUrl)` returns the DataURL if cached. If cached as DataURL, `iconSrc` is a data: URL. When the `<img>` receives a data: URL, `onLoad` fires synchronously in some browsers, but React schedules the state update. This causes a flash.\n\nAlso, for DataURL src: `fetchAndCacheIcon` is only called after `onLoad`. The FIRST render always has `imgLoaded=false`. The `onLoad` event then fires and `setImgLoaded(true)` is called. This causes a re-render with `opacity: 1`.\n\nThe REAL FIX: We should initialize `imgLoaded` to `true` if the icon is ALREADY in the cache (as a DataURL), so no skeleton/opacity flash happens.\n\n```tsx\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) return false;\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  return cached != null; // If we have a data: URL cached, image is "already loaded"\n});\n```\n\nAdditionally, when `iconSrc` changes (in the `useEffect` for `item.iconUrl` change), we should check if the new URL is cached:\n\n```tsx\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  if (cached) {\n    setIconSrc(cached);\n    setImgLoaded(true); // Already have it cached, no delay\n  } else {\n    setImgLoaded(false);\n    setIconSrc(item.iconUrl);\n  }\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nBut there\'s STILL the issue of the FIRST render on remount. Even with the init state fix, the component remounts and `useState(() => ...)` DOES initialize correctly. So if the cache has the DataURL, `imgLoaded` starts as `true`. This would fix the flash.\n\nHOWEVER: there\'s another issue. After `fetchAndCacheIcon` stores the DataURL in the cache, the NEXT time the component mounts, `getIconCache` returns the DataURL. So `imgLoaded` initializes to `true`. The image starts with `opacity: 1`. No delay!\n\nBut the FIRST time the component mounts (before `fetchAndCacheIcon` has run), `getIconCache` returns `null`, so `imgLoaded = false`. The `onLoad` fires, `setImgLoaded(true)`.\n\nFor SUBSEQUENT mounts (after page switch / after drag), `getIconCache` returns the cached DataURL, and `imgLoaded = true` from the start. But `iconSrc` is also the DataURL. So the image is shown immediately!\n\nWait, but there\'s a subtlety: when `iconSrc` is a DataURL, the `<img src={dataUrl}>` is set, and `onLoad` fires after the component renders. Before `onLoad` fires, the image has `opacity: 0` (since `imgLoaded = false` on initial state).\n\nWith my fix: `imgLoaded` starts as `true` if cached. So `opacity: 1` from the start. And `iconSrc` is the DataURL. The image displays immediately! ✓\n\nThis fixes the delay for cached icons.\n\nBUT: what about the `useEffect` that runs on mount (line 38-43)?\n\n```tsx\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  setImgLoaded(false); // ← THIS RESETS imgLoaded to false!\n  setIconSrc(getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl);\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nThis `useEffect` runs after mount AND whenever `item.iconUrl` changes. On INITIAL MOUNT, `item.iconUrl` matches the initial state, so this effect runs and resets `imgLoaded = false`!\n\nThis is the ROOT CAUSE of the delay: even if `imgLoaded` was initialized to `true`, the `useEffect` on mount immediately resets it to `false`.\n\nThe fix: the `useEffect` should only run when `item.iconUrl` CHANGES (not on initial mount). Or better: it should only reset `imgLoaded` if the URL actually changed.\n\nFIX APPROACH:\n1. Initialize `imgLoaded` to `true` if icon is cached\n2. Use `useRef` to track previous `item.iconUrl` and only reset if it actually changed\n3. Don\'t run the effect on mount if the URL is the same as initial\n\nBetter approach:\n```tsx\nconst prevIconUrlRef = useRef(item.iconUrl);\n\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (item.iconUrl === prevIconUrlRef.current && prevIconUrlRef.current !== undefined) return; // Skip if unchanged\n  // Actually this doesn\'t work for mount...\n```\n\nActually the simplest fix: move the `useEffect` logic to use a `useRef` to skip the first mount:\n\n```tsx\nconst initialMountRef = useRef(true);\n\nuseEffect(() => {\n  if (initialMountRef.current) {\n    initialMountRef.current = false;\n    return; // Skip initial mount - state already initialized correctly\n  }\n  // Only reset on actual URL change\n  if (!item.iconUrl) { setIconSrc(undefined); setImgError(false); setImgLoaded(false); return; }\n  setImgError(false);\n  const cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl);\n  setImgLoaded(cached != null); // true if cached, false if not\n  setIconSrc(cached ?? item.iconUrl);\n}, [item.iconUrl]);\n```\n\nThis way:\n- On initial mount: skip the effect, keep initialized state (which already checked cache)\n- On URL change: reset + check cache\n\nCombined with initializing `imgLoaded` from cache:\n```tsx\nconst [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() => {\n  if (!item.iconUrl) return false;\n  return getIconCache(item.iconUrl) != null;\n});\n```\n\nThis should fix the delay!\n\nActually, wait. Let me think more carefully. The useEffect runs after every render where `item.iconUrl` changed. On initial mount, it ALWAYS runs. So:\n\n1. Component mounts: `imgLoaded = true` (if cached) ← good\n2. React paints to DOM: image shows with opacity:1 ← good\n3. useEffect runs: `setImgLoaded(false)` ← bad, causes flash back to opacity:0\n4. onLoad fires: `setImgLoaded(true)` ← back to visible\n\nThis is EXACTLY the flash issue! The useEffect is resetting imgLoaded to false even though we just checked the cache.\n\nWith my fix using `initialMountRef`:\n1. Component mounts: `imgLoaded = true` (if cached)\n2. React paints: opacity:1 ← good\n3. useEffect runs: initialMountRef.current=true → skip → set to false → returns early\n4. NO FLASH ✓\n\nThen if `item.iconUrl` changes (user edits the item):\n5. useEffect runs: not initial mount → reset imgLoaded based on cache check ✓\n\nThis is the correct fix!\n\nLet me also think about whether there\'s any other source of delay:\n\nThe `iconSrc` state is initialized from:\n```tsx\n() => item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined\n```\n\nIf `getIconCache` returns a DataURL, `iconSrc = dataUrl`. Good.\nIf `getIconCache` returns null, `iconSrc = item.iconUrl` (remote URL). Need to load. Can\'t avoid delay for uncached icons.\n\nBut: when `iconSrc = dataUrl` and `imgLoaded = true`, the image shows immediately. ✓\nWhen `iconSrc = remoteUrl` and `imgLoaded = false`, the image shows after loading. Normal behavior.\n\nThe KEY insight: the `useEffect` was resetting `imgLoaded = false` on EVERY MOUNT, defeating the purpose of checking the cache in the initial state.\n\nSummary of fix for AppIcon:\n1. When URL changes: check cache for new URL to set imgLoaded correctly\n\nThis should eliminate all rendering delays for cached icons.\n\nOne more thing: for the `iconSrc` initialization, if `getIconCache` returns the DataURL, then `iconSrc = dataUrl`. But the useEffect (which we\'ll now skip on mount) also calls `setIconSrc(getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl)`. Since we\'re skipping it, `iconSrc` stays as the DataURL from initialization. ✓\n\nLet me now write the fix.\n', action=<ActionType.THINK: 'think'>)

<action>
**FileEditAction**
Path: [/workspace/app-ctg0jdeaugap/src/components/AppIcon.tsx]
Thought: 根因找到：`AppIcon` 每次重新挂载（翻页/拖拽后数据变化导致 unmount→remount）时，`imgLoaded` 初始化为 `false`，且 `useEffect` 无论是否是初次挂载都会再次 `setImgLoaded(false)` 覆盖缓存状态 → 即使图片已有 DataURL 缓存，也要等 `onLoad` 再次触发才变回可见。

**两处并行修复：**
1. `imgLoaded` 初始化时直接检查缓存（有缓存 → `true`，跳过骨架屏）

```
  const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
  // 有本地缓存（DataURL）时直接标记已加载，避免重新挂载时闪白
  const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() =>
    !!(item.iconUrl && getIconCache(item.iconUrl)),

  // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL

  // 标记是否为初次挂载：初次挂载时 state 已由 lazy initializer 正确初始化，不需要再重置
```

Here's the result of running `cat -n` on the file: /workspace/app-ctg0jdeaugap/src/lib/iconCache.ts:
     1 /**
     2  * 图标本地缓存模块
     3  * - 将远程图标 URL fetch 转为 base64 DataURL 存入 localStorage
     4  * - key: btoa(url) 截断，避免特殊字符
     5  * - 删除应用时调用 evictIconCache 清理孤儿缓存
     6  * - 存储上限 100 条，超出时 LRU 淘汰最旧条目
     7  */
     8 
     9 const CACHE_NS = 'icon_c:';
    10 const META_KEY = 'icon_c_meta'; // JSON: { [cacheKey]: timestamp }
    11 const MAX_ENTRIES = 100;
    12 
    13 function toCacheKey(url: string): string {
    14   // btoa 不支持多字节字符，先 encodeURIComponent 再 btoa
    15   try {
    16     return CACHE_NS + btoa(encodeURIComponent(url)).slice(0, 60);
    17   } catch {
    18     return CACHE_NS + url.slice(0, 60).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');
    19   }
    20 }
    21 
    22 function readMeta(): Record<string, number> {
    23   try {
    24     return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(META_KEY) || '{}');
    25   } catch {
    26     return {};
    27   }
    28 }
    29 
    30 function saveMeta(meta: Record<string, number>): void {
    31   try {
    32     localStorage.setItem(META_KEY, JSON.stringify(meta));
    33   } catch { /* ignore */ }
    34 }
    35 
    36 /** 从缓存读取图标 DataURL，未命中返回 null */
    37 export function getIconCache(url: string): string | null {
    38   if (!url || url.startsWith('data:') || url.startsWith('blob:')) return null;
    39   try {
    40     return localStorage.getItem(toCacheKey(url));
    41   } catch {
    42     return null;
    43   }
    44 }
    45 
    46 /** 将 DataURL 写入缓存，超限时 LRU 淘汰 */
    47 export function setIconCache(url: string, dataUrl: string): void {
    48   if (!url || url.startsWith('data:') || url.startsWith('blob:')) return;
    49   const key = toCacheKey(url);
    50   const meta = readMeta();
    51 
    52   // 超限：移除最旧的条目
    53   const keys = Object.keys(meta);
    54   if (keys.length >= MAX_ENTRIES && !meta[key]) {
    55     const oldest = keys.sort((a, b) => meta[a] - meta[b]).slice(0, keys.length - MAX_ENTRIES + 1);
    56     for (const k of oldest) {
    57       try { localStorage.removeItem(k); } catch { /* ignore */ }
    58       delete meta[k];
    59     }
    60   }
    61 
    62   try {
    63     localStorage.setItem(key, dataUrl);
    64     meta[key] = Date.now();
    65     saveMeta(meta);
    66   } catch {
    67     // localStorage 空间不足时静默跳过
    68   }
    69 }
    70 
    71 /** 删除指定 URL 的缓存条目 */
    72 export function deleteIconCache(url: string): void {
    73   if (!url) return;
    74   const key = toCacheKey(url);
    75   try { localStorage.removeItem(key); } catch { /* ignore */ }
    76   const meta = readMeta();
    77   delete meta[key];
    78   saveMeta(meta);
    79 }
    80 
    81 /**
    82  * 清理孤儿缓存：遍历 meta，删除不在 validUrls 中的条目
    83  * 调用时机：整体数据重新加载后（importData / removeItem）
    84  */
    85 export function pruneIconCaches(validUrls: Set<string>): void {
    86   const meta = readMeta();
    87   const validKeys = new Set([...validUrls].map(toCacheKey));
    88   for (const k of Object.keys(meta)) {
    89     if (!validKeys.has(k)) {
    90       try { localStorage.removeItem(k); } catch { /* ignore */ }
    91       delete meta[k];
    92     }
    93   }
    94   saveMeta(meta);
    95 }
    96 
    97 /**
    98  * 异步 fetch 远程图标并缓存为 base64 DataURL。
    99  * - 已缓存 → 直接返回缓存
   100  * - fetch 失败 / CORS 阻断 → 返回 null（不影响显示）
   101  */
   102 export async function fetchAndCacheIcon(url: string): Promise<string | null> {
   103   if (!url) return null;
   104   if (url.startsWith('data:') || url.startsWith('blob:')) return url;
   105 
   106   const cached = getIconCache(url);
   107   if (cached) return cached;
   108 
   109   try {
   110     const resp = await fetch(url, { mode: 'cors', cache: 'force-cache' });
   111     if (!resp.ok) return null;
   112     const blob = await resp.blob();
   113     if (!blob.type.startsWith('image/')) return null;
   114 
   115     return await new Promise<string | null>((resolve) => {
   116       const reader = new FileReader();
   117       reader.onload = () => {
   118         const dataUrl = reader.result as string;
   119         setIconCache(url, dataUrl);
   120         resolve(dataUrl);
   121       };
   122       reader.onerror = () => resolve(null);
   123       reader.readAsDataURL(blob);
   124     });
   125   } catch {
   126     return null;
   127   }
   128 }
   129

AgentThinkAction(thought='The issue is that `getIconCache` uses `localStorage.getItem()` in the `useState` lazy initializer. This is called during React render. But `localStorage` operations are synchronous and can be slow, especially on mobile where localStorage reads can take milliseconds.\n\nMore importantly: the `getIconCache` function returns `null` for data: URLs and blob: URLs (line 38: `if (!url || url.startsWith(\'data:\') || url.startsWith(\'blob:\')) return null;`). So if `iconUrl` IS a data: URL (from a previous cache operation), `getIconCache` returns null, `imgLoaded` is false, and it has to wait for `onLoad`.\n\nBut the BIGGER issue is: `getIconCache` reads from `localStorage`. If the favicon was cached as a DataURL, localStorage would return the dataURL. But `localStorage` can be slow on mobile.\n\nActually, the REAL problem I introduced: the `initialMountRef` approach. When `item` prop changes (which happens when a drag operation repositions items), React might NOT unmount and remount the component - it REUSES the existing component with new props. In this case:\n\n1. Component has `item = A` (old item)\n2. Data updates → parent re-renders → `item = A\'` (same ID, different position)\n3. Component gets new props but does NOT remount (same key)\n4. `imgLoaded` = still `true` (from old state) ← GOOD\n5. `useEffect` for `item.iconUrl`: `initialMountRef.current = false` (already false) → runs the effect\n6. `cached = getIconCache(item.iconUrl)` → returns DataURL if cached\n7. `setImgLoaded(cached != null)` → if NOT yet cached (first load), sets to false! Then waits for onLoad\n\nBut wait, if the iconUrl didn\'t change, the useEffect doesn\'t run at all (deps haven\'t changed). That\'s fine.\n\nNow, the DRAG issue: when user drags an icon and drops it, the item\'s position changes. But its `iconUrl` doesn\'t change. So the `useEffect` does NOT run (deps unchanged). `imgLoaded` stays at whatever it was. ← This should be FINE.\n\nWAIT. The real problem might be something else entirely. Let me reconsider.\n\nWhen does `AppIcon` UNMOUNT and REMOUNT vs just RERENDER?\n- It unmounts/remounts when the `key` prop changes\n- It just rerenders when props change but `key` stays same\n\nIn Desktop.tsx, how are AppIcon instances keyed? Let me look at the grid rendering code.\n\nLooking at Desktop.tsx line 440+:\n```tsx\nfor (let c = 0; c < gridCols; c++) {\n  const item = pageItems.find((it) => it.row === r && it.col === c);\n```\n\nThe key for the cell is `${r}-${c}`. When an item MOVES from (row=0, col=0) to (row=1, col=2), the cell at (0,0) now shows a different item or empty, and cell at (1,2) shows the moved item.\n\nIf cell keys are `${r}-${c}`, then:\n- Cell (0,0) → key="0-0" → had itemA → now empty → AppIcon unmounts\n- Cell (1,2) → key="1-2" → was empty → now has itemA → AppIcon MOUNTS fresh\n\nFresh mount → `imgLoaded` initialized from `getIconCache`. If cached → `true`, if not → `false`.\n\nThe localStorage-based cache should have the icon if it was previously loaded. So on fresh mount, `imgLoaded` should be `true` for already-seen icons. ← This is what v53 fixed.\n\nBut the user says "延迟更严重了" - delay got WORSE. Why?\n\nThe issue could be: `getIconCache` reads from `localStorage` which is synchronous but SLOW. The lazy initializer runs during React\'s rendering phase. If `getIconCache` takes time (due to localStorage), it slows down the initial render.\n\nBut more importantly: the `initialMountRef` fix introduced a REGRESSION. Here\'s the scenario:\n\n1. AppIcon mounts with item (iconUrl = "https://example.com/favicon.ico")\n2. `imgLoaded` = false (not cached yet - localStorage doesn\'t have it)\n3. `iconSrc` = "https://example.com/favicon.ico"\n4. useEffect runs: `initialMountRef.current = true → set false, SKIP` ← Correct\n5. Browser fetches the image\n6. `onLoad` fires → `setImgLoaded(true)` → `fetchAndCacheIcon(iconUrl)` called (fire-and-forget)\n7. `fetchAndCacheIcon` ASYNC fetches the icon, converts to DataURL, stores in localStorage\n\n8. Later: component unmounts (page change or drag)\n9. Component remounts: `imgLoaded = getIconCache(item.iconUrl) != null`\n\nWait - `fetchAndCacheIcon` is async. It might not have finished storing the cache by the time the component remounts. If the user switches pages quickly (within < 1-2 seconds), the cache may not be written yet.\n\nActually I think the bigger issue is a different one. Let me look at the `onLoad` handler again:\n\n```tsx\nonLoad={() => {\n  setImgLoaded(true);\n  // 图片加载成功后，后台静默缓存为 DataURL；不修改 iconSrc 避免 src 变动闪白\n  if (!item.iconUrl || iconSrc.startsWith(\'data:\')) return;\n  fetchAndCacheIcon(item.iconUrl); // fire-and-forget，下次挂载时从缓存读取\n}}\n```\n\nWhen `imgLoaded` is `true` (cached case) and `iconSrc` is a DataURL:\n- The `<img>` has `opacity: imgLoaded ? 1 : 0` = `opacity: 1`\n- But `imgLoaded` is `true` from state initializer, NOT from `onLoad` firing\n- When the `<img src={dataUrl}>` renders and loads, `onLoad` still fires\n- But `imgLoaded` is already `true`, so `setImgLoaded(true)` is a no-op\n\nThis seems fine. Let me think about what could make things WORSE...\n\nOH. I think I found it. The `initialMountRef` is a `useRef`, which means it persists across re-renders of the SAME component instance. But when an item CHANGES (different item renders in the same cell), the `initialMountRef.current` might still be `false` (from the previous item\'s "initial mount" skip).\n\nScenario:\n1. Cell (0,0) mounts with itemA (iconUrl = urlA)\n2. `initialMountRef.current = true` (newly mounted)\n3. useEffect runs: `initialMountRef.current = true → set false, SKIP`\n4. itemA\'s image loads, `imgLoaded = true`\n\n5. Drag: itemA moves to (1,2), itemB moves to (0,0)\n6. Cell (0,0) now has itemB (different item, SAME component instance reused by React since key="0-0" unchanged)\n7. `imgLoaded` is STILL `true` from itemA (React didn\'t remount, just rerender with new props)\n8. `initialMountRef.current` is `false` (set in step 3)\n9. `item.iconUrl` changes from urlA to urlB → useEffect runs\n10. useEffect: `initialMountRef.current = false` → NOT initial mount → runs the effect\n11. `cached = getIconCache(urlB)` \n12. If urlB IS cached: `setImgLoaded(true)`, `setIconSrc(dataUrl)` ← Fast!\n13. If urlB is NOT cached: `setImgLoaded(false)`, `setIconSrc(urlB)` ← Shows shimmer\n\nThis is the correct behavior! For uncached icons, there will be a shimmer. For cached, immediate display.\n\nBut what about `imgLoaded = true` from itemA while waiting for itemB\'s image to load? In step 9-13, we correctly set `imgLoaded = false` if not cached. So the image starts invisible while loading. This seems correct.\n\nActually wait, in step 7: `imgLoaded = true` (from itemA). If itemB\'s URL is different, we go through the useEffect (step 9-13). If cached: we set `imgLoaded = true` and `iconSrc = dataUrl`. The image stays at `opacity: 1` the whole time... BUT there\'s a brief moment where `imgLoaded = true` but `iconSrc` is still the OLD dataUrl (itemA\'s cached URL). \n\nReact batches state updates in useEffect. `setImgLoaded` and `setIconSrc` are called together in the effect (lines 49-50). React 18 batches these into a single re-render. So the image source and loaded state update atomically. ← Fine.\n\nHmm. Actually let me reconsider the whole approach.\n\nThe REAL root issue: `getIconCache` reads from localStorage. localStorage reads are synchronous blocking calls on the main thread. On mobile:\n- Reading a small item (< 100KB) takes ~0.1ms\n- Reading a large DataURL (> 100KB per icon) could take ~1-5ms per read\n\nIf we have 16 icons on a page, that\'s 16 × localStorage reads on each page mount. Each read happens during React render (lazy initializers run during render). This could be ~50ms of synchronous blocking work.\n\nBut wait, was this always the case? Even though the image already loaded via the `<img>` tag, we\'re fetching it AGAIN via `fetch()` API with `mode: \'cors\'`. This second fetch might fail due to CORS if the server doesn\'t allow it!\n\nAnd if it fails → `fetchAndCacheIcon` returns null → nothing cached → next time also no cache → always delayed!\n\nTHIS is the likely reason icons never get cached!\n\nThe fix: instead of doing a second fetch, we should cache the image from the already-loaded `<img>` element. We can use Canvas to convert the `<img>` to a DataURL:\n\n```tsx\nonLoad={(e) => {\n  setImgLoaded(true);\n  if (!item.iconUrl || iconSrc.startsWith(\'data:\')) return;\n  // Use canvas to convert already-loaded img to DataURL (no second network request)\n  try {\n    const img = e.currentTarget;\n    const canvas = document.createElement(\'canvas\');\n    canvas.width = img.naturalWidth || img.width;\n    canvas.height = img.naturalHeight || img.height;\n    const ctx = canvas.getContext(\'2d\');\n    if (ctx) {\n      ctx.drawImage(img, 0, 0);\n      const dataUrl = canvas.toDataURL(\'image/png\');\n      setIconCache(item.iconUrl, dataUrl);\n      // Also update iconSrc to use cached version for next render\n    }\n  } catch {\n    // CORS-tainted canvas → can\'t use toDataURL, fall back to fetchAndCacheIcon\n    fetchAndCacheIcon(item.iconUrl);\n  }\n}}\n```\n\nBut using canvas has the same CORS issue! If the image is cross-origin without CORS headers, the canvas will be tainted and `toDataURL()` will throw a SecurityError.\n\nHmm. Elements LATER in the DOM stack ABOVE earlier elements (within the same stacking context). The shimmer comes first in DOM, the img comes second → img is on TOP of shimmer. ✓\n\nBUT: the img needs to have `position: relative` to create a stacking context and stack above the absolute shimmer. Then it\'s drawn AFTER the shimmer in DOM order, which means it\'s on top.\n\nWith:\n```tsx\nshimmer: position: absolute, inset: 0 (fills container)  \nimg: position: static (normal flow), w-full h-full (fills container due to size)\n```\n\nThe img in normal flow will be positioned AFTER the shimmer (in document flow). But in stacking contexts, absolute elements are painted between background and normal flow elements. So the img (normal flow) paints ON TOP of shimmer (absolute). ✓\n\nThis should work! The shimmer is always there but covered by the img once loaded.\n\nBUT: there\'s one more issue. When `imgLoaded` was used to control opacity, the benefit was: on cached images, the img showed immediately at full opacity. Without imgLoaded, the img ALWAYS shows at opacity:1. But for a very brief moment (1 frame), the container shows the shimmer AND the img. If the img src is a dataUrl (instant), this is invisible.\n\nFor remote URLs on first load: shimmer shows, then img appears on top once loaded.   // 有本地缓存（DataURL）时直接标记已加载，避免重新挂载时闪白
```
  const [imgLoaded, setImgLoaded] = useState(() =>
    !!(item.iconUrl && getIconCache(item.iconUrl)),
  );
```

```
  const [imgError, setImgError] = useState(false);
  // 优先使用本地缓存的 DataURL，无缓存时使用远程 URL
  const [iconSrc, setIconSrc] = useState<string | undefined>(() =>
    item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined
  );

  // 用 ref 记录上次 iconUrl，useEffect 只在 iconUrl 真正变化时才更新 iconSrc（跳过初次挂载）
  const prevIconUrlRef = useRef(item.iconUrl);

  // item.iconUrl 变化时（编辑后）同步更新 iconSrc；初次挂载时 prevIconUrlRef === item.iconUrl → 跳过
  useEffect(() => {
    if (prevIconUrlRef.current === item.iconUrl) return;
    prevIconUrlRef.current = item.iconUrl;
    setImgError(false);
    setIconSrc(item.iconUrl ? (getIconCache(item.iconUrl) ?? item.iconUrl) : undefined);
  }, [item.iconUrl]);
```

AgentThinkAction(thought='The user says: hover-merge to folder is broken - items get position-swapped BEFORE the hover delay completes. This means when the user drags an icon over another icon, instead of waiting 800ms to merge into a folder, it immediately swaps positions when they lift their finger.\n\nThe root issue: in `onUp`, when `targetItemId` is set (pointer is over another icon), the code calls `swap()` immediately. But if the user was INTENDING to trigger a hover-merge (by holding over the icon for 800ms), and the merge timer hasn\'t fired yet when they lift finger, the `onUp` handler calls swap instead.\n\nThe fix: in `onUp`, if a merge timer is pending (i.e., the user was hovering over the same item for < 800ms), we should NOT swap - we should just leave both items in place. The swap should only happen if there was NO pending merge intent.\n\nOR: better approach - if the user lifts their finger within the 800ms window, treat it as a regular swap. Only if they held for 800ms+, treat it as a merge.\n\nActually wait - re-reading the user\'s complaint: "在悬停前就已经完成了位置交换" = "position swap happens BEFORE hover completes". This means:\n1. User drags icon A over icon B\n2. Before 800ms elapses, the swap happens\n3. The merge never gets triggered\n\nWhen does the swap happen? In `onUp`. If the user lifts their finger, `onUp` fires, finds a cell with `data-cell` and `data-itemid = B.id`, then calls swap.\n\nThe problem is: there\'s no way to know if the user INTENDED to merge (long hover) vs swap (quick drag and drop). On mobile, users typically just drop the icon - they\'re not trying to hold for 800ms.\n\nActually, re-reading the complaint more carefully: "悬停合并文件夹功能失效" = "hover-merge to folder feature is non-functional". Combined with "在悬停前就已经完成了位置交换" = "position swap completes before hovering".\n\nI think the user means: they TRY to hover over an icon (intending to merge), but a position swap happens IMMEDIATELY (or too quickly). The merge timer (800ms) never fires because the swap happens first on `onUp`.\n\nThe design question: should dropping on an icon (lifting finger immediately) do a SWAP? Or should it require a long hover to merge and a quick drop to swap?\n\nLooking at real iOS behavior: on iOS, dragging over another icon MERGES them into a folder. There\'s no "swap" behavior when dropping on another icon - it always merges. But this app has added a swap feature for quick drops.\n\nThe user seems to want: hover for 800ms → merge; quick drop → swap. But the current behavior is: quick drop → swap (which happens before the 800ms merge can trigger).\n\nI think the user wants PURE MERGE behavior: dragging over another app icon should ALWAYS try to merge (after a delay), NOT swap. The swap should only happen when dropping on an EMPTY cell.\n\nBut then again, "swap" is a useful feature for rearranging icons.\n\nActually, looking at the code flow in `onUp`:\n- If `targetItemId` is set AND `targetItemId !== g.source.itemId`, we call `swap()`\n- The merge timer may be running in the background (800ms)\n\nWhen the user lifts their finger at 0-799ms while over icon B:\n1. `onUp` fires\n2.
